 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-70a95e129e6f40e51925c045d8d1ac1f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1910" data-rawheight="1834" data-original-token="v2-70a95e129e6f40e51925c045d8d1ac1f" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-2408b66d7461a8e66ad372c79a49c4f2_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1910" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-70a95e129e6f40e51925c045d8d1ac1f_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="we2IWXJZ">准备了淀粉水，等会要用。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-36a3d9ab99672e574b81c0bdcf85f7cb_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1792" data-rawheight="1651" data-original-token="v2-36a3d9ab99672e574b81c0bdcf85f7cb" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-4cf723d3c04f56457d365cefda8b9a22_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1792" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-36a3d9ab99672e574b81c0bdcf85f7cb_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="sVhdvKXg">茄子炒成虎皮状就盛出来。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-d31f98f5acbd477264696833e5e59651_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1799" data-rawheight="1259" data-original-token="v2-d31f98f5acbd477264696833e5e59651" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-6385a08f7743cc4efe4e5b8e081fa11d_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1799" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-d31f98f5acbd477264696833e5e59651_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="JC72EmT8">蒜和辣椒煸一下出香味。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-7eb009bf58346a765f6c89a35de599b0_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1298" data-rawheight="1084" data-original-token="v2-7eb009bf58346a765f6c89a35de599b0" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-4502f0909e9f67ff9ef48a5b8c6f54ea_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1298" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-7eb009bf58346a765f6c89a35de599b0_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 <p data-pid="nJm9uQ8O">放解好冻的肉沫。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-41b39361501655e3b13e84b78efb3d48_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2048" data-rawheight="1585" data-original-token="v2-41b39361501655e3b13e84b78efb3d48" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-8aec5912ed3ea626216003f67d253b95_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2048" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-41b39361501655e3b13e84b78efb3d48_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="0JViPt8b">油脂煸出来，放黄豆酱，没有黄豆酱就放豆瓣酱。</p>

  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-2fe8c676e6319e98f7ce087580371172_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1592" data-rawheight="2048" data-original-token="v2-2fe8c676e6319e98f7ce087580371172" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-9c126f076dfae68160096809d46da21c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1592" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-2fe8c676e6319e98f7ce087580371172_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 <p data-pid="ZNUYaDWb">倒入茄子炒啊炒。</p>

 <p data-pid="ptefr7N2">倒入淀粉水炒啊炒。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-54e8014f6fc8435c7f37c84b038c4803_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1429" data-rawheight="1295" data-original-token="v2-54e8014f6fc8435c7f37c84b038c4803" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-068d0e021b34175d623fd5ba30f6fd34_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1429" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-54e8014f6fc8435c7f37c84b038c4803_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 <p data-pid="XqZdUS7O">香喷喷的，颜色不错吧。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-98d9e4d4298e3f10efe7de148156408f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2128" data-rawheight="1785" data-original-token="v2-98d9e4d4298e3f10efe7de148156408f" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-4e8887ffbeb635856f8ae1a43cb0d5c8_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2128" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-98d9e4d4298e3f10efe7de148156408f_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="3s0VWu8f">肉沫茄子完成啦。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-fdbb085803ee39b262e69ba313f677eb_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1259" data-rawheight="881" data-original-token="v2-fdbb085803ee39b262e69ba313f677eb" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-b42ca0bf6355cb50a984dc26d78bc67f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1259" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-fdbb085803ee39b262e69ba313f677eb_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="QjHQCG6l">开始做香菇炒肉啦。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-39dcdd27dffcb9c361a37840e97e25b7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1600" data-rawheight="1084" data-original-token="v2-39dcdd27dffcb9c361a37840e97e25b7" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-64a0edea0857f7d8e82212e9d7ba973a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-39dcdd27dffcb9c361a37840e97e25b7_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="Tl7WR1EM">也是放蒜和辣椒。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-01c48145ec9df939e5fccb93161072aa_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1791" data-rawheight="1210" data-original-token="v2-01c48145ec9df939e5fccb93161072aa" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-5c69212398cefecb8f6495593f74368d_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1791" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-01c48145ec9df939e5fccb93161072aa_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="H39eWr5J">然后放腌好了的肉片。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-262889bffdb1fab17c97c98075b3ffe5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1708" data-rawheight="1569" data-original-token="v2-262889bffdb1fab17c97c98075b3ffe5" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-807c6f0470638708a036096e8fc2131b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1708" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-262889bffdb1fab17c97c98075b3ffe5_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="JPOYqpZd">因为有淀粉，所以炒的时候，手感滑溜溜的，也不粘锅。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-e897a0b56d2c6a39189ff225aa724712_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1735" data-rawheight="1322" data-original-token="v2-e897a0b56d2c6a39189ff225aa724712" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-3dddbd47d4685b04d6867c1577de9a24_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1735" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e897a0b56d2c6a39189ff225aa724712_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="ZkYEpadU">上次有人竟然说我饭量大，其实我是吃两顿啦，晚上吃不完的，明天中午热一下就可以吃了，比较方便。所以不准说我饭量大呜呜～</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-1b08588788ad24147d633c8fe7bdc200_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1684" data-rawheight="1251" data-original-token="v2-1b08588788ad24147d633c8fe7bdc200" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-d258ffe2bd2b5147b69c5be0afc4d1cf_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1684" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-1b08588788ad24147d633c8fe7bdc200_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="hAhjsGPo">对了我这个锅也不大的…</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-5a469aaf0c13e4dc5acbdf95c7f66b7b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2048" data-rawheight="1998" data-original-token="v2-5a469aaf0c13e4dc5acbdf95c7f66b7b" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-39998212012d2ea5b12ae0791badea29_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2048" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-5a469aaf0c13e4dc5acbdf95c7f66b7b_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="zQm2QUTl">两个馒头，我爱吃馒头。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-f9b1d8aba3176fd9dc00e5eb76428fb0_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2048" data-rawheight="1947" data-original-token="v2-f9b1d8aba3176fd9dc00e5eb76428fb0" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-1306e9ebc7a6c8acf64931f56db24c1f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2048" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-f9b1d8aba3176fd9dc00e5eb76428fb0_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="ZuCfhHLV">做好啦，吃饭饭。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-89f898687d786817f3db69c618c31e85_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2048" data-rawheight="1761" data-original-token="v2-89f898687d786817f3db69c618c31e85" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-e035b9dc4caaacd9b0bc4840f866a308_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2048" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-89f898687d786817f3db69c618c31e85_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="D02QMqOz">每盘一张独照。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-4457285863ab2cfafbdac3ff86dabd24_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2048" data-rawheight="1718" data-original-token="v2-4457285863ab2cfafbdac3ff86dabd24" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-4b81e96fb5624cf2e4a1e588da4b9b5f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2048" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4457285863ab2cfafbdac3ff86dabd24_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>

 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-257079fda0874dfd3e0706df9f8656c1_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2025" data-rawheight="2048" data-original-token="v2-257079fda0874dfd3e0706df9f8656c1" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-da63162f279d11bc44d7ae7b57dcd237_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2025" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-257079fda0874dfd3e0706df9f8656c1_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="NSTc02th">很不错，不愧是我，肉末茄子很香，不枉我伤了手。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-dea2e36a4d2c79b2faf7baf3d7c581a7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1280" data-rawheight="2585" data-original-token="v2-dea2e36a4d2c79b2faf7baf3d7c581a7" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-84a8f48ec794e40fb6cb6bca1c5edf5a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1280" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-dea2e36a4d2c79b2faf7baf3d7c581a7_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="GD5scNwS">吃饭辣，明天见。</p>
 <p data-pid="b3mUpTIb">————</p>
 <p data-pid="4y_pfttc">3月21日更新</p>
 <p data-pid="65g9yNsj">大家晚上好啊～</p>
 <p data-pid="FYTnkNR3">最近网络上出现的新闻挺多的，我看着有些闹心、愤怒、无力，没错，最多的感受就是无奈。对于普通人来讲，所有引起社会公愤的新闻，终将以无奈收尾。评论区里我们找共鸣，现实里其实还是一个人。</p>
 <p data-pid="YY_U7WHa">我想说的是，注重自身，活在当下，定要开心。这实践起来不简单，但我们要先有这个信念。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-7a744d7d5990b6933de9deaebb4bdfbb_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1803" data-rawheight="1351" data-original-token="v2-7a744d7d5990b6933de9deaebb4bdfbb" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1803" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-7a744d7d5990b6933de9deaebb4bdfbb_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="K5Igry8T">你看我，穷且没工作，但我还是吃吃喝喝呀</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-440cf496b65d7bee5bc0b4463441079e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2106" data-rawheight="1280" data-original-token="v2-440cf496b65d7bee5bc0b4463441079e" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2106" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-440cf496b65d7bee5bc0b4463441079e_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="QcEj3hWw">我之前很省，你们说不能太省，尤其是吃的方面，于是我听了，就开始不在吃的方面太抠了，我不买那些乱七八糟不实用的东西啦。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-7963000a1862ff4c07fa8fa54828ab64_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="922" data-rawheight="975" data-original-token="v2-7963000a1862ff4c07fa8fa54828ab64" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="922" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7963000a1862ff4c07fa8fa54828ab64_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="KiWcp-CL">于是，我更快乐了。没错，吃，也是一种快乐。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-aa6a793160b3ec2caaee09b2a6e38a81_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1369" data-rawheight="2048" data-original-token="v2-aa6a793160b3ec2caaee09b2a6e38a81" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1369" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-aa6a793160b3ec2caaee09b2a6e38a81_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="ieBlfLmx">不止是知友，最近开了公众号，公众号里的朋友也给我提意见，让我在抖音也开账号，这样或许可以带货挣钱，大家是真的都知道我拮据这件事了</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-3ee4341cb5de670225cb2938e94f73e6_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2048" data-rawheight="1609" data-original-token="v2-3ee4341cb5de670225cb2938e94f73e6" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2048" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-3ee4341cb5de670225cb2938e94f73e6_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="yL3ODCVY">我的主要收入还是靠做自媒体，但做自媒体收入很低，我最近在想别的办法，实在不行就在家做兼职。加油！</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-d638b544aef013224757aef5d6557c7a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="3014" data-rawheight="1280" data-original-token="v2-d638b544aef013224757aef5d6557c7a" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="3014" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-d638b544aef013224757aef5d6557c7a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="573E0MWM">很多人问我，你不觉得孤单吗？我觉得我现在有资格回答这个问题了。</p>
 <p data-pid="tm4eL19N">常年在外打工漂泊的朋友，独自一人拼搏的朋友：孤单是一整天做自己感兴趣的事；孤单是一整天学习看书学技能且无人打扰；孤单是不用拆开一板哇哈哈，自己独占四瓶的乐趣。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-f9443e15178471ea444699cfac7caabe_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2009" data-rawheight="1832" data-original-token="v2-f9443e15178471ea444699cfac7caabe" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2009" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-f9443e15178471ea444699cfac7caabe_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="sTa947I3">这样看来，孤单不过就是一个人做自己爱做的、喜欢做的事。你可以感受到落寞，反过来你也可以感受到自由。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-69dcb26e687fbedf2fbc94fe4c425248_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1280" data-rawheight="2051" data-original-token="v2-69dcb26e687fbedf2fbc94fe4c425248" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1280" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-69dcb26e687fbedf2fbc94fe4c425248_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="TCV8m7zV">我可能是那个喜欢独处的人，所以不觉得太孤单，常觉自由。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-7bfeaca1ddb9bf300675d6e9bb4355d4_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1280" data-rawheight="2900" data-original-token="v2-7bfeaca1ddb9bf300675d6e9bb4355d4" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1280" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-7bfeaca1ddb9bf300675d6e9bb4355d4_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="RpodKm9N">我发明了一个新菜哈哈哈。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-e5b4949fd59f368f1723dce17e753710_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2014" data-rawheight="2048" data-original-token="v2-e5b4949fd59f368f1723dce17e753710" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2014" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-e5b4949fd59f368f1723dce17e753710_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="fEQxYkby">莲藕炒肉，真的很好吃～</p>
 <p data-pid="Q31DuuK4">下面是简单的小步骤：</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-0da2a52eee443f251a3cf03e5235b290_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1212" data-rawheight="1084" data-original-token="v2-0da2a52eee443f251a3cf03e5235b290" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1212" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-0da2a52eee443f251a3cf03e5235b290_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="A4g0Z4ZQ">放油。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-a0b6ca2e731f72437eeb2c32e2f61f13_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1696" data-rawheight="1515" data-original-token="v2-a0b6ca2e731f72437eeb2c32e2f61f13" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1696" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-a0b6ca2e731f72437eeb2c32e2f61f13_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="3HgdHeeo">油热放姜、大蒜</p>
 <p data-pid="b4MitvFh">（ps：我最近特别喜欢大蒜，因为炒菜真的很香～非常加分）</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-7d40a3f658d8d7392feb9f13d31c9835_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1039" data-rawheight="1108" data-original-token="v2-7d40a3f658d8d7392feb9f13d31c9835" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1039" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-7d40a3f658d8d7392feb9f13d31c9835_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="IWkIB7Rg">五花肉偏肥的地方切成片，放进去煸出油。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-3c38f7d86cd5214912214c24603247ca_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2048" data-rawheight="1565" data-original-token="v2-3c38f7d86cd5214912214c24603247ca" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2048" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-3c38f7d86cd5214912214c24603247ca_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="gGHF40vv">煸到五花肉边边有点卷起来的样子。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-f4983945664a5291e81e893bbb253dc0_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1918" data-rawheight="1491" data-original-token="v2-f4983945664a5291e81e893bbb253dc0" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1918" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-f4983945664a5291e81e893bbb253dc0_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="G3V-Lmsp">放切成小块的莲藕，对了莲藕是用削皮刀削过皮的。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-8db88c25374590db5657d5b2bd2029bb_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1725" data-rawheight="1625" data-original-token="v2-8db88c25374590db5657d5b2bd2029bb" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1725" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-8db88c25374590db5657d5b2bd2029bb_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="vxhF4UgS">我放了老抽、生抽、一点盐，颜色好看吧哈哈</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-a73f7e0444839cc7de418262b942473c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1339" data-rawheight="1253" data-original-token="v2-a73f7e0444839cc7de418262b942473c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1339" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a73f7e0444839cc7de418262b942473c_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="ldzGX1-Q">油大一点会更诱人，你们可以试试炒出来颜色真的很好看。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-d0123865588a59f82f54e9adf0458044_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1849" data-rawheight="1585" data-original-token="v2-d0123865588a59f82f54e9adf0458044" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1849" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-d0123865588a59f82f54e9adf0458044_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="oQ3mOtbT">木耳可以不用放，我放是因为它在冰箱里好几天了，再不吃就不好吃了</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-52c04e2d41e1812fc889242fd60e19a0_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2042" data-rawheight="1963" data-original-token="v2-52c04e2d41e1812fc889242fd60e19a0" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2042" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-52c04e2d41e1812fc889242fd60e19a0_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="mm6wVPlg">颜色真好看啊，偷吃了一口。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-83b6fc902cf87647f4928ed06dc628e6_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2048" data-rawheight="1822" data-original-token="v2-83b6fc902cf87647f4928ed06dc628e6" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2048" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-83b6fc902cf87647f4928ed06dc628e6_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="z_AfDY29">第二道菜是平菇炒肉。</p>
 <p data-pid="wglyZp4e">这个平菇真的超级大，必须拍给你们看一下。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-164cac0eb42511a030ad919a55329caf_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1818" data-rawheight="2048" data-original-token="v2-164cac0eb42511a030ad919a55329caf" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1818" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-164cac0eb42511a030ad919a55329caf_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="C2dakfPb">切好的肉和辣椒，又出现了姜、大蒜。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-c5d046e025019cbb5a8be4a559989aa1_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1770" data-rawheight="1347" data-original-token="v2-c5d046e025019cbb5a8be4a559989aa1" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1770" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-c5d046e025019cbb5a8be4a559989aa1_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="ydLcCuhB">油脂一定要中火煸出来，这样会让肉有焦香味。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-1658aec413cc9ed8990685b897cce3ce_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1450" data-rawheight="1507" data-original-token="v2-1658aec413cc9ed8990685b897cce3ce" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1450" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-1658aec413cc9ed8990685b897cce3ce_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="hoGvEgSw">平菇撕成条状，放进去。这里我放了盐，还放了酱油。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-0b2b35e4044c5f1448f9f98c7d7d6a8c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1280" data-rawheight="2192" data-original-token="v2-0b2b35e4044c5f1448f9f98c7d7d6a8c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1280" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0b2b35e4044c5f1448f9f98c7d7d6a8c_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="TNMCpw7c">晚餐两道菜完成啦。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-88445c6fb57cec10f4ab3a6b2d0a9519_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1951" data-rawheight="2041" data-original-token="v2-88445c6fb57cec10f4ab3a6b2d0a9519" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1951" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-88445c6fb57cec10f4ab3a6b2d0a9519_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="OXRHtDeW">讲真，平菇比肉好吃。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-802b1b511bfd1d48a22632e0a802df51_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1769" data-rawheight="2048" data-original-token="v2-802b1b511bfd1d48a22632e0a802df51" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1769" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-802b1b511bfd1d48a22632e0a802df51_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="8UXxTPLz">近照，馋一下你们</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-74f7d07b944e8f98d1fd46ef2181e12f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1916" data-rawheight="2048" data-original-token="v2-74f7d07b944e8f98d1fd46ef2181e12f" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1916" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-74f7d07b944e8f98d1fd46ef2181e12f_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="vai8V4GM">莲藕炒肉，我又发现了宝藏菜肴，为自己点个赞</p>
 <p data-pid="ygk1Btdx">————</p>
 <p data-pid="RD818r5n">3月23日更新</p>
 <p data-pid="gc8y8a7l">现在外面正在下雨☔️，淅淅沥沥的，躺在床上更新真的好爽呀～</p>
 <p data-pid="eR8kMqp4">今天下午出去逛了一会儿，天气非常热，完全属于夏天了，不知道你们所在的城市天气如何？前两天冷到穿棉服，今天热到穿短袖，也是神了。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-09aed559c6b98b52219f80305f888548_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1759" data-rawheight="1975" data-original-token="v2-09aed559c6b98b52219f80305f888548" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1759" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-09aed559c6b98b52219f80305f888548_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="1t754C1p">这不得吃个冰淇淋降温一下，四块钱还好不贵，香草味的，很好吃。老板没有给我勺子，我蹭得只想回出租屋，走的飞快，找了个树荫处坐下来，打开才发现我这个傻子没有要勺子。还好盖子够硬。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-1807f4a2ee012c881593b0623d757044_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1995" data-rawheight="2048" data-original-token="v2-1807f4a2ee012c881593b0623d757044" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1995" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-1807f4a2ee012c881593b0623d757044_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="BDK91HGk">还别说，这“勺子”还挺能舀的。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-eb6af83d030248cd373242e46b8fc2a2_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2048" data-rawheight="2046" data-original-token="v2-eb6af83d030248cd373242e46b8fc2a2" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2048" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-eb6af83d030248cd373242e46b8fc2a2_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="CwFYAdYr">口香糖是和冰淇淋一起买的，四个2块钱。选了三种口味，草莓、西瓜、葡萄。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-fb25071d7e67dbe2a4054925a1f7ff9e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1983" data-rawheight="2048" data-original-token="v2-fb25071d7e67dbe2a4054925a1f7ff9e" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1983" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-fb25071d7e67dbe2a4054925a1f7ff9e_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="AMr9uXad">打开后，还是熟悉的样子。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-24009a0d55c7bd7220bb7108a60dad04_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2048" data-rawheight="2046" data-original-token="v2-24009a0d55c7bd7220bb7108a60dad04" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2048" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-24009a0d55c7bd7220bb7108a60dad04_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="Wz-T-C-7">咱这么大了，就别来小孩那套了。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-b124344a372a4d340b305aa8b809730d_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2121" data-rawheight="2119" data-original-token="v2-b124344a372a4d340b305aa8b809730d" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2121" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b124344a372a4d340b305aa8b809730d_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="c5x3UtFv">这小花小时候天天摘，摘很多放在河里，觉得可美了。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-616f1bfce818fa2e34cd845ed5306bb2_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="717" data-rawheight="717" data-original-token="v2-616f1bfce818fa2e34cd845ed5306bb2" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="717" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-616f1bfce818fa2e34cd845ed5306bb2_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="P0usvCTF">回家的路是真长，中午没吃什么东西，见到路边小摊我还是没忍住诱惑。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-92aa4a2df2784f7178daf0c2b1aa67fa_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="922" data-rawheight="1306" data-original-token="v2-92aa4a2df2784f7178daf0c2b1aa67fa" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="922" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-92aa4a2df2784f7178daf0c2b1aa67fa_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="DaHS4Q0m">虽然它臭，但它是真香啊啊啊</p>
 <p data-pid="9F4_-b0r">大概吃了几口就开始下雨了。淅淅沥沥的一会儿下得很大，一会儿又不下了。我是喜欢雨的，所以如果不是很大的话，我是不会躲雨的。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-87cc8e693546cb145b4d2cb84c992ce5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1155" data-rawheight="572" data-original-token="v2-87cc8e693546cb145b4d2cb84c992ce5" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1155" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-87cc8e693546cb145b4d2cb84c992ce5_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="yWnYj7O0">雨还在下，我已经成功回到出租屋了，躺着…本想看看我抖音的粉丝有几个了，没想到一刷刷了一个多小时…嗐，手机的奴隶呀～</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-fedad35bd0c05bc3e2ac8538a918924b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1280" data-rawheight="2772" data-original-token="v2-fedad35bd0c05bc3e2ac8538a918924b" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1280" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-fedad35bd0c05bc3e2ac8538a918924b_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="Rxf6_mj5">做个晚餐，这是细面条。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-764c3628f9dd3fd5f957b899d069a1a9_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1372" data-rawheight="1399" data-original-token="v2-764c3628f9dd3fd5f957b899d069a1a9" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1372" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-764c3628f9dd3fd5f957b899d069a1a9_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="GV9yg6tc">因为不想洗菜板，所以就直接用剪刀剪了蘑菇。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-c376a38625c727ad31ec57af74401959_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2048" data-rawheight="1881" data-original-token="v2-c376a38625c727ad31ec57af74401959" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2048" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c376a38625c727ad31ec57af74401959_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="-oTMfQfj">放进去炒一下。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-59e733ad766c1e709f9b602f03cb3fd4_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1960" data-rawheight="1850" data-original-token="v2-59e733ad766c1e709f9b602f03cb3fd4" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1960" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-59e733ad766c1e709f9b602f03cb3fd4_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="QpTRh65k">加水，昨天在小店里没吃完打包回来的汤，里面有肉、菜，统统倒进去。</p>
 <p data-pid="Xh6xw6he">我现在又养成了一个习惯，就是打包，不管是什么吃不完就打包，打包回来就又有了一顿。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-7d62d4b4354ad3de3bab4b2fade313b6_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1823" data-rawheight="1823" data-original-token="v2-7d62d4b4354ad3de3bab4b2fade313b6" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1823" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7d62d4b4354ad3de3bab4b2fade313b6_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="371X7GW7">煮……</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-c49d4fb19c6a5ec2768b2a8a817b3c78_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2048" data-rawheight="2046" data-original-token="v2-c49d4fb19c6a5ec2768b2a8a817b3c78" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2048" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-c49d4fb19c6a5ec2768b2a8a817b3c78_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="69SgCreZ">煮开加面条，我这个面条非常容易熟。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-bc1af6fd0b4fb5a7e467ba4fd745887a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1729" data-rawheight="1728" data-original-token="v2-bc1af6fd0b4fb5a7e467ba4fd745887a" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1729" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-bc1af6fd0b4fb5a7e467ba4fd745887a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="Hv2YQg9V">不用加盐，直接出锅。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-afaec9a8a7d3a374576e1c465fd81ab9_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2048" data-rawheight="1768" data-original-token="v2-afaec9a8a7d3a374576e1c465fd81ab9" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2048" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-afaec9a8a7d3a374576e1c465fd81ab9_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="o-IsumgL">剩的汤打包回来不要扔+水+面条=好吃便宜不浪费且方便容易的晚餐哦～</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-967bde344193e488c6c4d48776793f60_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="2269" data-rawheight="1280" data-original-token="v2-967bde344193e488c6c4d48776793f60" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2269" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-967bde344193e488c6c4d48776793f60_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="WxIox53Y">今天一天的饭量，吃吃喝喝又是一天，不过我也是在努力做自媒体中…虽然不成功，但普通人都是在无数个不成功中度过的，敬普通人。</p>
